    function onLinkDropdownChange(e){
        var selValue = document.getElementById("dropdown-null").value;
        var countryList = document.getElementById("country-list").innerHTML = '';
        var nameArr = selValue.split(',');
        nameArr.forEach(function (item) {
            var ul = document.getElementById('country-list');
            let li = document.createElement('li');
            ul.appendChild(li)
            var element = document.createElement("a");
            var a = li.appendChild(element)
            a.innerHTML += item;
            a.setAttribute('href',item);
            });
        }
